============================================================================\n# EDITOR MANAGER\n# ============================================================================\n\nclass EditorManager:\n    """Manages active editor instances"""\n    \n    def __init__(self):\n        self.editors: Dict[str, Dict[str, Any]] = {}\n    \n    def create_editor(self, editor_type: str, user_id: int, **kwargs) -> str:\n        """Create a new editor instance"""\n        import uuid\n        editor_id = str(uuid.uuid4())\n        \n        self.editors[editor_id] = {\n            "editor_id": editor_id,\n            "editor_type": editor_type,\n            "user_id": user_id,\n            "created_at": datetime.utcnow(),\n            "last_modified": datetime.utcnow(),\n            "is_modified": False,\n            **kwargs\n        }\n        \n        return editor_id\n    \n    def get_editor(self, editor_id: str) -> Optional[Dict[str, Any]]:\n        """Get editor by ID"""\n        return self.editors.get(editor_id)\n    \n    def update_editor(self, editor_id: str, **kwargs):\n        """Update editor data"""\n        if editor_id in self.editors:\n            self.editors[editor_id].update(kwargs)\n            self.editors[editor_id]["last_modified"] = datetime.utcnow()\n            self.editors[editor_id]["is_modified"] = True\n    \n    def delete_editor(self, editor_id: str):\n        """Delete editor instance"""\n        if editor_id in self.editors:\n            del self.editors[editor_id]\n    \n    def list_editors(self, user_id: int) -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:\n        """List all editors for a user"""\n        return [\n            editor for editor in self.editors.values()\n            if editor["user_id"] == user_id\n openMonacoEditor(apiClient: APIClient) {\n    try {\n        // Get language selection\n        const languages = await apiClient.get(\'/api/v1/editors/monaco/languages\');\n        const languageItems = languages.languages.map((lang: any) => ({\n            label: lang.name,\n            description: lang.extensions.join(\', \'),\n            id: lang.id\n        }));\n        \n        const selectedLanguage = await vscode.window.showQuickPick(languageItems, {\n            placeHolder: \'Select programming language\'\n        });\n        \n        if (!selectedLanguage) {\n            return;\n        }\n        \n        // Get theme selection\n        const theme = await vscode.window.showQuickPick(\n            [\n                { label: \'Dark Theme\', value: \'vs-dark\' },\n                { label: \'Light Theme\', value: \'vs-light\' }\n            ],\n            { placeHolder: \'Select editor theme\' }\n        );\n        \n        if (!theme) {\n            return;\n        }\n        \n        // Open editor\n        const response = await apiClient.post(\'/api/v1/editors/monaco/open\', {\n            language: selectedLanguage.id,\n            theme: theme.value,\n            content: \'// Start coding here...\\n\'\n        });\n        \n        // Create webview panel\n        const panel = vscode.window.createWebviewPanel(\n            \'monacoEditor\',\n            `Monaco Editor - ${selectedLanguage.label}`,\n            vscode.ViewColumn.One,\n            {\n                enableScripts: true,\n                retainContextWhenHidden: true\n            }\n        );\n        \n        panel.webview.html = getMonacoEditorHTML(response, selectedLanguage.id, theme.value);\n        \n        // Handle messages from webview\n        panel.webview.onDidReceiveMessage(\n            async message => {\n                switch (message.command) {\n                    case \'save\':\n                        await saveMonacoFile(apiClient, response.editor_id, message.content);\n                        break;\n                    case \'close\':\n                        await apiClient.delete(`/api/v1/editors/${response.editor_id}`);\n                        panel.dispose();\n                        break;\n                }\n            }\n        );\n        \n        vscode.window.showInformationMessage(`Monaco Editor opened: ${response.editor_id}`);\n        \n    } catch (error: any) {\n        vscode.window.showErrorMessage(`Failed to open Monaco editor: ${error.message}`);\n    }\n}\n\n/**\n * Open file in Monaco editor\n */\nasync function openFileInMonaco(apiClient: APIClient, uri: vscode.Uri) {\n    try {\n        const filePath = uri.fsPath;\n        const ext = path.extname(filePath);\n        \n        // Detect language from extension\n        const languageMap: { [key: string]: string } = {\n            \'.py\': \'python\',\n            \'.js\': \'javascript\',\n            \'.ts\': \'typescript\',\n            \'.html\': \'html\',\n            \'.css\': \'css\',\n            \'.json\': \'json\',\n            \'.yaml\': \'yaml\',\n            \'.yml\': \'yaml\',\n            \'.md\': \'markdown\',\n            \'.java\': \'java\',\n            \'.go\': \'go\',\n            \'.rs\': \'rust\',\n            \'.cpp\': \'cpp\',\n            \'.c\': \'c\',\n            \'.rb\': \'ruby\',\n            \'.php\': \'php\'\n        };\n        \n        const language = languageMap[ext] || \'plaintext\';\n        \n        // Open editor with file\n        const response = await apiClient.post(\'/api/v1/editors/monaco/open\', {\n            file_path: filePath,\n            language: language,\n            theme: \'vs-dark\'\n        });\n        \n        // Create webview panel\n        const panel = vscode.window.createWebviewPanel(\n            \'monacoEditor\',\n            `Monaco Editor - ${path.basename(filePath)}`,\n            vscode.ViewColumn.One,\n            {\n                enableScripts: true,\n                retainContextWhenHidden: true\n            }\n        );\n        \n        panel.webview.html = getMonacoEditorHTML(response, language, \'vs-dark\');\n        \n        // Handle messages\n        panel.webview.onDidReceiveMessage(\n            async message => {\n                switch (message.command) {\n                    case \'save\':\n                        await saveMonacoFile(apiClient, response.editor_id, message.content, filePath);\n                        vscode.window.showInformationMessage(\'File saved successfully\');\n                        break;\n                    case \'close\':\n                        await apiClient.delete(`/api/v1/editors/${response.editor_id}`);\n                        panel.dispose();\n                        break;\n                }\n            }\n        );\n        \n    } APIClient,\n    editorId: string,\n    content: string,\n    filePath?: string\n) {\n    try {\n        if (!filePath) {\n            // Ask for file path\n            const uri = await vscode.window.showSaveDialog({\n                filters: {\n                    \'All Files\': [\'*\']\n                }\n            });\n            \n            if (!uri) {\n                return;\n            }\n            \n            filePath = uri.fsPath;\n        }\n        \n        await apiClient.post(\'/api/v1/editors/monaco/save\', {\n            editor_id: editorId,\n            file_path: filePath,\n            content: content,\n            create_backup: true\n        });\n        \n        vscode.window.showInformationMessage(\'File saved successfully\');\n        \n    } catch (error: any) {\n        vscode.window.showErrorMessage(`Failed to save file: ${error.message}`);\n    }\n}\n\n/**\n * Open image editor\n */\nasync function openImageEditor(apiClient: APIClient) {\n    try {\n        // Get canvas size\n        const width = await vscode.window.showInputBox({\n            prompt: \'Enter canvas width\',\n            value: \'800\',\n            validateInput: (value) => {\n                const num = parseInt(value);\n                return isNaN(num) || num <= 0 ? \'Please enter a valid number\' : null;\n            }\n        });\n        \n        if (!width) {\n            return;\n        }\n        \n        const height = await vscode.window.showInputBox({\n            prompt: \'Enter canvas height\',\n            value: \'600\',\n            validateInput: (value) => {\n                const num = parseInt(value);\n                return isNaN(num) || num <= 0 ? \'Please enter a valid number\' : null;\n            }\n        });\n        \n        if (!height) {\n            return;\n        }\n        \n        // Open editor\n        const response = await apiClient.post(\'/api/v1/editors/image/open\', {\n            width: parseInt(width),\n            height: parseInt(height)\n        });\n        \n        // Create webview panel\n        const panel = vscode.window.createWebviewPanel(\n            \'imageEditor\',\n            \'Image Editor\',\n            vscode.ViewColumn.One,\n            {\n                enableScripts: true,\n                retainContextWhenHidden: true\n            }\n           switch (message.command) {\n                    case \'export\':\n                        await exportImage(apiClient, response.editor_id, message.format);\n                        break;\n                    case \'close\':\n                        await apiClient.delete(`/api/v1/editors/${response.editor_id}`);\n                        panel.dispose();\n                        break;\n                }\n            }\n        );\n        \n        vscode.window.showInformationMessage(\'Image editor opened\');\n        \n    } catch (error: any) {\n  \n    } catch (error: any) {\n        vscode.window.showErrorMessage(`Failed to export image: ${error.message}`);\n    }\n}\n\n/**\n * Open website builder\n */\nasync function List all active editors\n */\nasync function listEditors(apiClient: APIClient) {\n    try {\n        const response = await apiClient.get(\'/api/v1/editors/list\');\n        \n        if (response.total === 0) {\n            vscode.window.showInformationMessage(\'No active editors\');\n            return;\n        }\n        \n        const items = response.editors.map((editor: any) => ({\n            label: `${editor.editor_type} - ${editor.editor_id}`,\n            description: editor.file_path || \'No file\',\n            detail: `Created: ${new Date(editor.created_at).toLocaleString()}`,\n            editor: editor\n        }));\n        \n        const selected = await vscode.window.showQuickPick(items, {\n            placeHolder: \'Select an editor to manage\'\n        });\n        \n        if (!selected) {\n            return;\n        }\n        \n        // Show editor actions\n        const action = await vscode.window.showQuickPick(\n            [\n                { label: \'View Info\', value: \'info\' },\n                { label: \'Close Editor\', value: \'close\' }\n            ],\n            { placeHolder: \'Select action\' }\n        );\n        \n        if (!action) {\n            return;\n        }\n        \n        if (action.value === \'info\') {\n            const info = await apiClient.get(`/api/v1/editors/${selected.editor.editor_id}`);\n            vscode.window.showInformationMessage(\n                `Editor: ${info.editor_type}\\nCreated: ${new Date(info.created_at).toLocaleString()}\\nModified: ${info.is_modified}`\n            );\n        } else if (action.value === \'close\') {\n            await apiClient.delete(`/api/v1/editors/${selected.editor.editor_id}`);\n            vscode.window.showInformationMessage(\'Editor closed\');\n        }\n        \n    } catch (error: any) {\n        vscode.window.showErrorMessage(`Failed to list editors: ${error.message}`);\n    }\n}\n\n// ============================================================================\n// HTML GENERATORS\n// ============================================================================\n\nfunction getMonacoEditorHTML(response: any, language: string, theme: string): string {\n    return `<!DOCTYPE html>\n    <html>\n    <head>\n        <meta charset="UTF-8">\n        <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0">\n        <title>Monaco Editor</title>\n        <link rel="stylesheet" href="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/monaco-editor@0.44.0/min/vs/editor/editor.main.css">\n        <style>\n            body { margin: 0; padding: 0; overflow: hidden; }\n            #container { width: 100vw; height: 100vh; }\n            #toolbar {\n                background: #1e1e1e;\n                padding: 10px;\n                display: flex;\n                gap: 10px;\n                border-bottom: 1px solid #333;\n            }\n            button {\n                background: #0e639c;\n                color: white;\n                border: none;\n                padding: 8px 16px;\n                cursor: pointer;\n                border-radius: 4px;\n            }\n            button:hover { background: #1177bb; }\n            #editor { height: calc(100vh - 50px); }\n        </style>\n    </head>\n    <body>\n        <div id="container">\n            <div id="toolbar">\n                <button onclick="save()">Save</button>\n                <button onclick="close()">Close</button>\n                <span style="color: white; margin-left: auto; padding: 8px;">\n                    Lines: ${response.line_count} | Characters: ${response.character_count}\n                </span>\n            </div>\n            <div id="editor"></div>\n        </div>\n        \n        <script src="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/monaco-editor@0.44.0/min/vs/loader.js"></script>\n        <script>\n            const vscode = acquireVsCodeApi();\n            let editor;\n            \n            require.config({ paths: { vs: \'https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/monaco-editor@0.44.0/min/vs\' }});\n            \n            require([\'vs/editor/editor.main\'], function() {\n                editor = monaco.editor.create(document.getElementById(\'editor\'), {\n                    value: ${JSON.stringify(response.content)},\n                    language: \'${language}\',\n                    theme: \'${theme}\',\n                    automaticLayout: true,\n                    minimap: { enabled: true },\n                    fontSize: 14,\n                    lineNumbers: \'on\',\n                    scrollBeyondLastLine: false\n                });\n            });\n            \n            function save() {\n                vscode.postMessage({\n                    command: \'save\',\n                    content: editor.getValue()\n                });\n            }\n            \n            function close() {\n                vscode.postMessage({ command: \'close\' });\n            }\n        </script>\n    </body>\n    </html>`;\n}\n\nfunction getImageEditorHTML(response: any): string {\n    return `<!DOCTYPE html>\n    <html>\n    <head>\n        <meta charset="UTF-8">\n        <title>Image Editor</title>\n        <script src="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/fabric.js/5.3.0/fabric.min.js"></script>\n        <style>\n            body { margin: 0; padding: 0; font-family: Arial, sans-serif; }\n            #toolbar {\n                background: #2d2d2d;\n                padding: 10px;\n                display: flex;\n                gap: 10px;\n                border-bottom: 1px solid #444;\n            }\n            button {\n                background: #0e639c;\n                color: white;\n                border: none;\n                padding: 8px 16px;\n                cursor: pointer;\n                border-radius: 4px;\n            }\n            button:hover { background: #1177bb; }\n            #canvas-container {\n                display: flex;\n                justify-content: center;\n                align-items: center;\n                height: calc(100vh - 60px);\n                background: #1e1e1e;\n            }\n        </style>\n    </head>\n    <body>\n        <div id="toolbar">\n            <button onclick="addRectangle()">Rectangle</button>\n            <button onclick="addCircle()">Circle</button>\n            <button onclick="addText()">Text</button>\n            <button onclick="exportImage(\'png\')">Export PNG</button>\n            <button onclick="exportImage(\'jpg\')">Export JPG</button>\n            <button onclick="closeEditor()">Close</button>\n        </div>\n        <div id="canvas-container">\n            <canvas id="canvas" width="${response.width}" height="${response.height}"></canvas>\n        </div>\n        \n        <script>\n            const vscode = acquireVsCodeApi();\n            const canvas = new fabric.Canvas(\'canvas\', {\n                backgroundColor: \'#ffffff\'\n            });\n            \n            function addRectangle() {\n                const rect = new fabric.Rect({\n                    left: 100,\n                    top: 100,\n                    fill: \'#0e639c\',\n                    width: 100,\n                    height: 100\n                });\n                canvas.add(rect);\n            }\n            \n            function addCircle() {\n                const circle = new fabric.Circle({\n                    left: 150,\n                    top: 150,\n                    fill: \'#1177bb\',\n                    radius: 50\n                });\n                canvas.add(circle);\n            }\n            \n            function addText() {\n                const text = new fabric.IText(\'Edit me\', {\n                    left: 200,\n                    top: 200,\n                    fontSize: 24,\n                    fill: \'#000000\'\n                });\n                canvas.add(text);\n            }\n            \n            function exportImage(format) {\n                vscode.postMessage({\n                    command: \'export\',\n                    format: format,\n                    data: canvas.toDataURL(\'image/\' + format)\n                });\n            }\n            \n            function closeEditor() {\n                vscode.postMessage({ command: \'close\' });\n \n    def __init__(self):\n        self.editors: Dict[str, Dict[str, Any]] = {}\n    \n    def create_editor(self, editor_type: str, user_id: int, **kwargs) -> str:\n        """Create a new editor instance"""\n        editor_id = str(uuid.uuid4())\n        self.editors[editor_id] = {\n            "editor_id": editor_id,\n            "editor_type": editor_type,\n            "user_id": user_id,\n            "created_at": datetime.utcnow(),\n            "last_modified": datetime.utcnow(),\n            "is_modified": False,\n            **kwargs\n        }\n        return editor_id\n    \n    def get_editor(self, editor_id: str) -> Optional[Dict[str, Any]]:\n        """Get editor by ID"""\n        return self.editors.get(editor_id)\n    \n    def update_editor(self, editor_id: str, **kwargs):\n        """Update editor data"""\n        if editor_id in self.editors:\n            self.editors[editor_id].update(kwargs)\n            self.editors[editor_id]["last_modified"] = datetime.utcnow()\n            self.editors[editor_id]["is_modified"] = True\n    \n    def delete_editor(self, editor_id: str):\n        """Delete editor instance"""\n        if editor_id in self.editors:\n            del self.editors[editor_id]\n```\n\n### Monaco Editor HTML\n\n```html\n<!DOCTYPE html>\n<html>\n<head>\n    <link rel="stylesheet" {'role': 'assistant', 'content': '<function_calls>\n<create-file file_path="itechsmart-ninja/backend/app/integrations/github_client.py">\n"""\nGitHub Client - Comprehensive GitHub API integration\nProvides repository operations, PR management, issue tracking, and more\n"""\n\nfrom typing import List, Optional, Dict, Any, Tuple\nfrom datetime import datetime\nimport requests\nimport base64\nfrom enum import Enum\nimport logging\n\nlogger = logging.getLogger(__name__)\n\n\nclass GitHubAuthType(str, Enum):\n    """GitHub authentication types"""\n    PERSONAL_ACCESS_TOKEN = "pat"\n    OAUTH = "oauth"\n    APP = "app"\n\n\nclass PullRequestState(str, Enum):\n    """Pull request states"""\n    OPEN = "open"\n    CLOSED = "closed"\n    ALL = "all"\n\n\nclass IssueState(str, Enum):\n    """Issue states"""\n    OPEN = "open"\n    CLOSED = "closed"\n    ALL = "all"\n\n\nclass ReviewState(str, Enum):\n    """Pull request review states"""\n    APPROVED = "APPROVED"\n    CHANGES_REQUESTED = "CHANGES_REQUESTED"\n    COMMENTED = "COMMENTED"\n\n\nclass GitHubClient:\n    """\n    Comprehensive GitHub API client\n    \n    Features:\n    - Repository operations (clone, pull, push, fork)\n    - Pull request management (create, review, merge)\n    - Issue tracking (create, update, close)\n    - Branch management (create, delete, merge)\n    - Commit history (view, search, analyze)\n    - Code review automation\n    - GitHub Actions integration\n    - Webhook support\n    """\n    \n    def __init__(\n        self,\n        token: str,\n        auth_type: GitHubAuthType = GitHubAuthType.PERSONAL_ACCESS_TOKEN,\n        base_url: str = "https://api.github.com"\n    ):\n        """\n        Initialize GitHub client\n        \n        Args:\n            token: GitHub authentication token\n            auth_type: Type of authentication\n            base_url: GitHub API base URL\n        """\n        self.token = token\n        self.auth_type = auth_type\n        self.base_url = base_url\n        self.session = requests.Session()\n        self.session.headers.update({\n            "Authorization": f"token {token}",\n            "Accept": "application/vnd.github.v3+json",\n            "User-Agent": "iTechSmart-Ninja"\n        })\n    \n    def _request(\n        self,\n        method: str,\n        endpoint: str,\n        params: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = None,\n        json: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = None,\n        headers: Optional[Dict[str, str]] = None\n    ) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n        """\n        Make API request with error handling\n        \n        Args:\n            method: HTTP method\n            endpoint: API endpoint\n            params: Query parameters\n            json: JSON body\n            headers: Additional headers\n            \n        Returns:\n            Response data\n        """\n        url = f"{self.base_url}{endpoint}"\n        \n        try:\n            response = self.session.request(\n                method=method,\n                url=url,\n                params=params,\n                json=json,\n                headers=headers or {}\n            )\n            response.raise_for_status()\n            \n            # Handle rate limiting\n            if response.status_code == 429:\n                reset_time = int(response.headers.get(\'X-RateLimit-Reset\', 0))\n                logger.warning(f"Rate limit exceeded. Resets at {reset_time}")\n                raise Exception(f"Rate limit exceeded. Try again after {reset_time}")\n            \n            return response.json() if response.content else {}\n            \n        except requests.exceptions.HTTPError as e:\n            logger.error(f"GitHub API error: {e}")\n            raise Exception(f"GitHub API error: {e}")\n        except Exception as e:\n            logger.error(f"Request failed: {e}")\n            raise\n    \n    def _paginate(\n        self,\n        endpoint: str,\n        params: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = None,\n        max_pages: int = 10\n    ) -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:\n        """\n        Paginate through API results\n        \n        Args:\n            endpoint: API endpoint\n            params: Query parameters\n            max_pages: Maximum pages to fetch\n            \n        Returns:\n            List of all results\n        """\n        results = []\n        page = 1\n        params = params or {}\n        params[\'per_page\'] = 100\n        \n        while page <= max_pages:\n            params[\'page\'] = page\n            data = self._request(\'GET\', endpoint, params=params)\n            \n            if not data:\n                break\n            \n            if isinstance(data, list):\n                results.extend(data)\n                if len(data) < 100:\n                    break\n            else:\n                results.append(data)\n                break\n            \n            page += 1\n        \n        return results\n    \n    # ========================================================================\n    # REPOSITORY OPERATIONS\n    # ========================================================================\n    \n    def get_repository(self, owner: str, repo: str) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n        """\n        Get repository information\n        \n        Args:\n            owner: Repository owner\n            repo: Repository name\n            \n        Returns:\n            Repository data\n        """\n        return self._request(\'GET\', f\'/repos/{owner}/{repo}\')\n    \n    def list_repositories(\n        self,\n        user: Optional[str] = None,\n        org: Optional[str] = None,\n        type: str = "all",\n        sort: str = "updated"\n    ) -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:\n        """\n        List repositories\n        \n        Args:\n            user: Username (for user repos)\n            org: Organization name (for org repos)\n            type: Repository type (all, owner, member)\n            sort: Sort by (created, updated, pushed, full_name)\n            \n        Returns:\n            List of repositories\n        """\n        if org:\n            endpoint = f\'/orgs/{org}/repos\'\n        elif user:\n            endpoint = f\'/users/{user}/repos\'\n        else:\n            endpoint = \'/user/repos\'\n        \n        params = {\'type\': type, \'sort\': sort}\n        return self._paginate(endpoint, params=params)\n    \n    def create_repository(\n        self,\n        name: str,\n        description: Optional[str] = None,\n        private: bool = False,\n        auto_init: bool = True\n    ) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n        """\n        Create a new repository\n        \n        Args:\n            name: Repository name\n            description: Repository description\n            private: Make repository private\n            auto_init: Initialize with README\n            \n        Returns:\n            Created repository data\n        """\n        data = {\n            \'name\': name,\n            \'description\': description,\n            \'private\': private,\n            \'auto_init\': auto_init\n        }\n        return self._request(\'POST\', \'/user/repos\', json=data)\n    \n    def fork_repository(self, owner: str, repo: str) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n        """\n        Fork a repository\n        \n        Args:\n            owner: Repository owner\n            repo: Repository name\n            \n        Returns:\n            Forked repository data\n        """\n        return self._request(\'POST\', f\'/repos/{owner}/{repo}/forks\')\n    \n    def delete_repository(self, owner: str, repo: str) -> bool:\n        """\n        Delete a repository\n        \n        Args:\n            owner: Repository owner\n            repo: Repository name\n            \n        Returns:\n            Success status\n        """\n        try:\n            self._request(\'DELETE\', f\'/repos/{owner}/{repo}\')\n            return True\n        except Exception:\n            return False\n    \n    # ========================================================================\n    # BRANCH OPERATIONS\n    # ========================================================================\n    \n    def list_branches(self, owner: str, repo: str) -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:\n        """\n        List repository branches\n        \n        Args:\n            owner: Repository owner\n            repo: Repository name\n            \n        Returns:\n            List of branches\n        """\n        return self._paginate(f\'/repos/{owner}/{repo}/branches\')\n    \n    def get_branch(self, owner: str, repo: str, branch: str) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n        """\n        Get branch information\n        \n        Args:\n            owner: Repository owner\n            repo: Repository name\n            branch: Branch name\n            \n        Returns:\n            Branch data\n        """\n        return self._request(\'GET\', f\'/repos/{owner}/{repo}/branches/{branch}\')\n    \n    def create_branch(\n        self,\n        owner: str,\n        repo: str,\n        branch: str,\n        from_branch: str = "main"\n    ) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n        """\n        Create a new branch\n        \n        Args:\n            owner: Repository owner\n            repo: Repository name\n            branch: New branch name\n            from_branch: Source branch\n            \n        Returns:\n            Created branch data\n        """\n        # Get source branch SHA\n        source = self.get_branch(owner, repo, from_branch)\n        sha = source[\'commit\'][\'sha\']\n        \n        # Create reference\n        data = {\n            \'ref\': f\'refs/heads/{branch}\',\n            \'sha\': sha\n        }\n        return self._request(\'POST\', f\'/repos/{owner}/{repo}/git/refs\', json=data)\n    \n    def delete_branch(self, owner: str, repo: str, branch: str) -> bool:\n        """\n        Delete a branch\n        \n        Args:\n            owner: Repository owner\n            repo: Repository name\n            branch: Branch name\n            \n        Returns:\n            Success status\n        """\n        try:\n            self._request(\'DELETE\', f\'/repos/{owner}/{repo}/git/refs/heads/{branch}\')\n            return True\n        except Exception:\n            return False\n    \n    def merge_branches(\n Press `Ctrl+Shift+P`\n2. Type "Review Pull"\n3. Select "iTechSmart: Review Pull Request"\n4. Enter repository (owner/repo)\n5. Enter PR number\n6. Choose review type:\n   - **Approve** - Approve the changes\n   - **Request Changes** - Request modifications\n   - **Comment** - Add comments without approval\n7. Enter review comment\n\n**API:**\n```bash\nPOST /api/v1/github/repos/owner/repo/pulls/123/reviews\n{\n  "body": "Looks good to me!",\n  "event": "APPROVED",\n  "comments": []\n}\n```\n\n### Merge Pull Request\n\n**API:**\n```bash\nPUT /api/v1/github/repos/owner/repo/pulls/123/merge\n{\n  "merge_method": "squash"\n}\n```\n\n**Merge Methods:**\n- `merge` - Create a merge commit\n- `squash` - Squash and merge\n- `rebase` - Rebase and merge\n\n---\n\n## üêõ Issue Tracking\n\n### List Issues\n\n**Terminal:**\n```bash\n> gh-issues owner/repo\n```\n\n**Command Palette:**\n1.
